FunctionDef/Hint/lib_CPGL_3DE8735B=Turns on/off Void cinematic mode for all players. Cinematic mode hides the normal gameplay UI.  When cinematic mode is turned on, the state of the gameplay UI is cached, and when cinematic mode is turned off, the state of the gameplay UI is restored from that cache.
